FROM `Content` AS `c`

) AS `t` ON `c`.`Id` = `t`.`IdContent`

SELECT `c`.`Id`, `t`.`IdContent`, `t`.`c`, `t`.`Title`, `t`.`Description`, `t`.`IdParentContent`, `t`.`Id`
FROM `Content` AS `c`
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT `p`.`IdContent`, FALSE AS `c`, `c0`.`Title`, `c0`.`Description`, `p`.`IdParentContent`, `c0`.`Id`
    FROM `ParentContent` AS `p`
    INNER JOIN `Content` AS `c0` ON `p`.`IdContent` = `c0`.`Id`
) AS `t` ON `c`.`Id` = `t`.`IdContent`
WHERE `c`.`IdContentType` = 1
ORDER BY `c`.`Id`, `t`.`IdContent`, `t`.`IdParentContent`, `t`.`Id`

SELECT `c`.`Id`, `c`.`Description`, `t0`.`IdContent`, `t0`.`c`, `t0`.`Title`, `t0`.`Description`, `t0`.`IdParentContent`, `t0`.`Id`, `t0`.`c0`, `t0`.`Title0`, `t0`.`IdContent0`, `t0`.`IdParentContent0`, `t0`.`Id0`
FROM `Content` AS `c`
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT `p`.`IdContent`, FALSE AS `c`, `c0`.`Title`, `c0`.`Description`, `p`.`IdParentContent`, `c0`.`Id`, `t`.`c` AS `c0`, `t`.`Title` AS `Title0`, `t`.`IdContent` AS `IdContent0`, `t`.`IdParentContent` AS `IdParentContent0`, `t`.`Id` AS `Id0`
    FROM `ParentContent` AS `p`
    INNER JOIN `Content` AS `c0` ON `p`.`IdContent` = `c0`.`Id`
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT FALSE AS `c`, `c1`.`Title`, `p0`.`IdContent`, `p0`.`IdParentContent`, `c1`.`Id`
        FROM `ParentContent` AS `p0`
        INNER JOIN `Content` AS `c1` ON `p0`.`IdContent` = `c1`.`Id`
    ) AS `t` ON `c0`.`Id` = `t`.`IdContent`
) AS `t0` ON `c`.`Id` = `t0`.`IdParentContent`
WHERE `c`.`IdContentType` = 1
ORDER BY `c`.`Id`, `t0`.`IdContent`, `t0`.`IdParentContent`, `t0`.`Id`, `t0`.`IdContent0`, `t0`.`IdParentContent0`, `t0`.`Id0`
